NFR-007: No sprint/roadmap imports.\n    10→\"\"\"\n    11→\n    12→from __future__ import annotations\n    13→\n    14→from pathlib import Path\n    15→\n    16→from .models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n    17→\n    18→\n    19→def gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    20→    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n    21→\n    22→    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    23→    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    24→    \"\"\"\n    25→    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n    26→\n    27→    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    28→    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n    29→        return True, None\n    30→\n    31→    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    32→    if not output_file.exists():\n    33→        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n    34→\n    35→    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    36→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    37→    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n    38→        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n    39→\n    40→    # LIGHT stops here\n    41→    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n    42→        return True, None\n    43→\n    44→    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    45→    lines = content.splitlines()\n    46→    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n    47→        return False, (\n    48→            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n    49→            f\"in {output_file}\"\n    50→        )\n    51→\n    52→    # steps\n            result.append(entry)\n            continue\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check all steps\n            all_pass = True\n            for s in entry:\n                if s.gate:\n                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n                    if not passed:\n                        all_pass = False\n                        break\n                else:\n                    all_pass = False\n                    break\n            if all_pass:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n            else:\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n        else:\n            # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n                found_failure = True\n                result.append(entry)\n                continue\n\n            if entry.gate:\n                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n                if passed:\n                    skipped += 1\n                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n                    continue\n            found_failure = True\n            result.append(entry)\n\n    if skipped > 0:\n        print(f\"[roadmap] Skipped {skipped} steps (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n\n    if not result:\n        print(\"[roadmap] All steps already pass gates.
